==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-08-25_17-38-50-HKUST RoboMaster Team ENTERPRIZE 2025 Recruitment Begins!.txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: HKUST RoboMaster Team ENTERPRIZE 2025 Recruitment Begins!
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-25 17:38:50
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: ece-ug-list-request@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

Dear all Engineering UG Students,



 



Are you looking for a place where you can transform lectures knowledge into working robots, a place you can have hands-on experience in full-cycle machine production, or a place you can immerse yourself in a vibrant tech atmosphere with a community of like-minded enthusiasts?



 



Come and join RoboMaster Team ENTERPRIZE!



 







 



Introduction to RoboMaster and ENTERPRIZE



RoboMaster is the world's first intelligent shooting robot competition organised by DJI. In the competition, red and blue teams each field seven robots with different functionalities and engage in tactical combat using first-person shooter (FPS) gameplay on a MOBA-style tower defence map.



HKUST RoboMaster team ENTERPRIZE represents the university in the RoboMaster University Series every year. We have won international regional championships and RoboMaster University League branch championships in past years. Since the establishment ten years ago, the team has accumulated a wealth of technical expertise and fostered a strong technical atmosphere.



What do we do at ENTERPRIZE?



Constructing a robot is an interdisciplinary project that requires the collaborative efforts of developers from multiple technical departments. In our team, we are divided into the following four technical departments, each of which plays a crucial role in the manufacturing and development process of the robot. Choose one to join based on your interests or expertise!



The Mechanical Department is responsible for designing robot blueprints using the 3D modelling software SolidWorks, then processing parts via 3D printing or CNC machine tools, and finally assembling the robot structure to complete the transition from blueprint to reality. During the mid-to-late stages of the season, the Mechanical Department iterates on the blueprints and performs regular maintenance and repairs based on the issues and requirements encountered when the Software and Algorithm Departments test the robot.



The Hardware Department is responsible for designing and drawing PCB circuit boards, selecting and soldering appropriate electronic components, and finally connecting the circuits on the robot. During the subsequent testing process by the Software and Algorithm Departments, the hardware design is iterated based on the stability issues and performance requirements encountered by the system, and regular maintenance and troubleshooting work is also carried out.



The Software Department is responsible for implementing serial communication and motion control to build a system of various modules on the robot by writing C++ programs on the STM32 microcontroller. Tasks such as controlling motors and other motion actuators to achieve flexible robot movement, or ensuring that bullets are fired at a stable speed are important jobs of Software Department. During the subsequent testing process conducted by the Algorithm Department, the program and parameters will be optimized and adjusted by the Software Department according to the requirements for control accuracy and response speed.



The Algorithm Department needs to process information collected by sensors such as cameras and lidar to let the robots perceive the surroundings, as if equipping the robots with 'vision' or 'perception', and thus automatically or semi-automatically complete various tasks on the battlefield. This allows the robots to strike opponents and activate buffs more quickly and accurately than when controlled manually by operators, and thereby gains an advantage on the battlefield for the team.



How to join?



Step 1: Scan the QR code on the poster or click the link https://ust.az1.qualtrics.com/jfe/form/SV_cHolyyw6yx5YB4G <https://ust.az1.qualtrics.com/jfe/form/SV_cHolyyw6yx5YB4G>  to register.



Step 2: Scan the QR code on the poster or click the link https://discord.gg/wdD853YK <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdiscord.gg%2FwdD853YK&data=05%7C02%7Cxlilv%40connect.ust.hk%7C75610ae60df5489bb13408dde3bb2800%7C6c1d415239d044ca88d9b8d6ddca0708%7C1%7C0%7C638917115300726768%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=42fovMHQLB5XfDZaFkxqsUIAHsamzUJmCzobELnejUo%3D&reserved=0>  to join our Discord server. ‰∏ªÈ¢ò: [Press Release] HKUST Thanks National Ministry for Vote of Confidence with Three State Key Labs
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-25 19:31:59
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: allug-list-request@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

 



 



	

If you can‚Äôt read this email, click here <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2Fnews%2Fhkust-thanks-national-ministry-vote-confidence-three-state-key-labs&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7Cbcb7dc8879b34b0e084e08dde3c8d90c%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638917173970086414%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=cZDkop7MbxAlvNydqpHYGQcDye9fCc92giNQkNKlhtc%3D&reserved=0>  



	

 



	

 <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2F&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7Cbcb7dc8879b34b0e084e08dde3c8d90c%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638917173970108670%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=A5YCl8Agux6Sur52ROj08EWZiKt90NoJiSsjY36uE4k%3D&reserved=0> 



	

	

HKUST Thanks National Ministry for Vote of Confidence with Three State Key Labs  



Dedicated to Promoting Research and Innovation in Neuroscience, Optoelectronics, and Climate Resilience of Coastal Cities   



	

2025-08-25



	



 <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2Fsites%2Fdefault%2Ffiles%2Fnews%2F23883%2F1_ed.JPG&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7Cbcb7dc8879b34b0e084e08dde3c8d90c%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638917173970119215%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=MnKO6N9pvqPYS3Q61HTiWpB4f0Xz7aRI81JhmxHpNgc%3D&reserved=0> 



	

A group photo at the plaque presentation ceremony with John LEE, HKSAR Chief Executive (first row, middle), YIN Hejun, Minister of Science and Technology of the People's Republic of China (first row, forth left), ZHOU Ji, Director of the LOCPG (first row, forth right), SUN Dong, Secretary for HK Innovation, Technology and Industry (first row, third right), alongside directors of the 15 State Key Laboratories and the presidents of representative universities, including those from HKUST: President Prof. Nancy IP (second row, fifth left), Prof. Charles NG Wang-Wai, Vice-President for Institutional Advancement, Director of SKLCRCC and CLP Holdings Professor of Sustainability (third row, third left), Prof. Kristiaan NEYTS, Director of SKLDOE and Professor in the Department of Electronic and Computer Engineering (first row, second left), and Prof. FAN Zhiyong, Co-Director of SKLDOE and Chair Professor in the Department of Electronic and Computer Engineering (third row, first left).



	



The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology (HKUST) today received plaques from YIN Hejun, Minister of the Ministry of Science and Technology (MOST) for its three State Key Laboratories (SKLs) at the Government Headquarters of the Hong Kong Special Administrative Region (HKSAR). HKUST sincerely thanks MOST, and the Hong Kong Innovation, Technology, and Industry Bureau (ITIB) for their continued trust and recognition of the University‚Äôs research efforts. In addition to the two renamed SKLs following restructuring ‚Äì the ‚ÄúState Key Laboratory of Nervous System Disorders (SKLNSD)‚Äù and the ‚ÄúState Key Laboratory of Displays and Opto-Electronics (SKLDOE)‚Äù ‚Äì HKUST will also collaborate with The Hong Kong Polytechnic University (PolyU) to establish a new ‚ÄúState Key Laboratory of Climate Resilience for Coastal Cities (SKLCRCC)‚Äù. The new lab aims to provide scientific and technological support to address national priorities such as coping with extreme weather and enhancing urban safety and disaster prevention capabilities.



MOST initiated the optimization and restructuring of SKLs in 2022 and approved the restructuring for 12 existing labs in early 2025, along with the establishment of three new ones (one of which is jointly built by two universities). All 15 SKLs officially became national-level scientific and technological innovation platforms on July 1 this year. HKUST has both fully retained all its existing SKLs and successfully obtained approval to establish a new one. 



Chief Executive John LEE of HKSAR, Minister Yin Hejun of MOST, Director ZHOU Ji of the Liaison Office of the Central People's Government in the HKSAR (LOCPG), and Secretary SUN Dong of the ITIB attended today‚Äôs plaque presentation ceremony and held a forum with the presidents of five local universities and the directors of the 15 SKLs. They discussed how Hong Kong can leverage its talented professionals, innovative research, and international environment to better support the nation‚Äôs innovation-driven development strategy.  Prof. Nancy IP, HKUST President and Director of the SKLNSD, Prof. Kristiaan NEYTS, Director of SKLDOE, Prof. FAN Zhiyong, Co-Director of the SKLDOE, and Prof. Charles NG, Co-Director of SKLCRCC, for this discussion and the subsequent plaque-awarding ceremony.



HKSAR Chief Executive John Lee stated, "Under the principle of 'one country, two systems', Hong Kong has the advantage of enjoying strong support of the motherland and being closely connected to the world and actively plays the role as a 'super connector' and 'super value-adder'. The SKLs in Hong Kong serve as an important platform for bringing together outstanding researchers from all over the world by establishing partnerships with top universities and research institutions at home and abroad, helping to build Hong Kong into a hub for international high-end talent."



MOST Minister Yin Hejun said that the establishment of 15 State Key Laboratories in Hong Kong reflects the nation's high recognition and full confidence in Hong Kong's scientific research capabilities, innovation capacity and development potential. It also represents the Central Government's ardent expectations and momentous mission for Hong Kong's scientific community. He hopes these laboratories will further strengthen their commitment to addressing the scientific challenges underlying national needs, and dare to explore uncharted territories at the frontiers of science and technology.



LOCPG Director Zhou Ji stated that a number of internationally renowned scholars and scientists have become new Hong Kong residents in recent years. He anticipates Hong Kong to better leverage its unique advantages by vigorously promoting the holistic development of education, science, and talent cultivation, and to attract and nurture more world-class talents and innovative teams through high-caliber research platforms and collaborative initiatives.



ITIB Secretary Prof. Sun Dong stated: "The HKSAR Government initiated the restructuring exercise of the State Key Laboratories in Hong Kong in late 2023, and MOST approved the restructuring of 15 SKLs in Hong Kong in January 2025. We hope the SKLs will closely align with the country‚Äôs major strategic needs, focus on the global technology frontier, and significantly enhance research and development standards. We also hope that they will fully leverage Hong Kong‚Äôs advantages as an international city to actively expand global research collaborations, and cultivate and attract top talent from around the world, thus contributing to the technological self-reliance of the country and the development of Hong Kong into an international innovation and technology centre.‚Äù



HKUST President Prof. Nancy Ip stated: ‚ÄúHKUST sincerely thanks the Central Government, MOST and the ITIB for their great trust and endorsement. The University has not only completed the restructuring of its existing State Key Laboratories but has also been granted approval to establish a new one ‚Äî a strong recognition of HKUST‚Äôs research strength. The restructured system offers clearer strategic positioning and a more systematic and comprehensive overall framework. The extension of the State Key Laboratory program and the National Engineering Research Centers to Hong Kong has significantly enhanced collaborative innovation between scientists from the mainland and Hong Kong. This enables Hong Kong to better leverage its distinctive advantages in research and international connectivity to serve national strategic priorities, while also providing a broader platform for its integration into the nation‚Äôs science and technology development. HKUST will continue to align with national strategic needs, commit to pioneering scientific research and breakthroughs in core technologies, foster interdisciplinary collaboration, attract top-tier talent globally, and contribute meaningfully to building China into a leading science and technology powerhouse and elevating Hong Kong‚Äôs role as an international innovation and technology hub.‚Äù



According to arrangements by the Innovation and Technology Commission, each laboratory will receive regular funding support, and the university will provide corresponding matching resources to a sustained focus on national priorities and the execution of long-term, strategic research missions. Each laboratory has developed clear development plans, performance targets and standardized operational and management mechanisms. 





Rooted in the National System, Building a High Ground for Innovation and Technology





HKUST‚Äôs three approved laboratories will focus on major national needs, conducting cutting-edge basic research and tackling key technologies:



The State Key Laboratory of Nervous System Disorders (formerly the ‚ÄúState Key Laboratory of Molecular Neuroscience‚Äù established in 2009), is Hong Kong‚Äôs first SKL in molecular neuroscience and the first SKL at HKUST. The laboratory conducts forward-looking fundamental and translational research, with major achievements like blood-based diagnostic technology for Alzheimer‚Äôs disease and a whole-brain gene-editing system. The laboratory has secured numerous research grants and cross-institutional collaboration programs. The laboratory successfully completed optimization and restructuring in February 2025. Its new direction after restructuring focuses on the mechanisms of neurological diseases, diagnostic and therapeutic methods, and the development of new technologies, integrating interdisciplinary teams and AI technologies to promote technology transfer and talent cultivation.



The State Key Laboratory of Displays and Opto-Electronics was approved in 2013. It is dedicated to promoting the innovative development of next-generation optoelectronic technologies, artificial intelligence, and advanced manufacturing to meet critical national needs in the related fields. It also facilitates technology transfer to the domestic high-tech industry and fosters exchanges in innovation and technology planning and talent development among the three regions in the Greater Bay Area. The Laboratory was approved to transition into the ‚ÄúState Key Laboratory of Displays and Optoelectronics‚Äù in February 2025, with new research areas including perovskite-based optoelectronic materials and devices, organic light-emitting devices, quantum dot‚Äìbased LEDs (QLEDs) and nanorods, augmented reality (AR) and extended reality (XR), 3D displays, thin-film transistor‚Äìbased flexible sensors, organic solar cells, and ultra-wideband semiconductors. 



The State Key Laboratory of Climate Resilience for Coastal Cities will be jointly established by HKUST and PolyU in 2025. It will focus on research areas such as extreme weather prediction, urban disaster prevention and mitigation, infrastructure resilience, and early disaster warning systems. The laboratory will fully leverage HKUST‚Äôs world-leading Geotechnical Centrifuge Facility, its international research network as well as the University‚Äôs strengths in the area and combine it with PolyU‚Äôs expertise in engineering and policy management to jointly address the challenges posed by climate change and promote the development of safe, green and sustainable coastal cities. 





New Laboratory Fosters Innovation Ecosystem and Leads Regional Collaboration





The newly added laboratory ‚Äì SKLCRCC - aims to strengthen scientific and technological research on comprehensive urban disaster prevention and mitigation, with the goal of ensuring public safety and urban green development. Related research projects will fully utilize HKUST‚Äôs internationally leading geotechnical centrifuge cluster testing platform. 



Hong Kong's innovation and technology ecosystem is increasingly mature. Facing the opportunities and challenges of the new era, HKUST will continue to deepen international collaboration and exchanges, jointly serve the broader national development strategy, become an innovation hub attracting top-tier talent from home and abroad, and inject new momentum into the development of the national science and technology endeavor.

About The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology 

The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology (HKUST) (https://hkust.edu.hk/ <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2F&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7Cbcb7dc8879b34b0e084e08dde3c8d90c%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638917173970204206%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=rh7hBwsNtM%2FB45L3Saa6uRHEg6IK1cLYx%2Fcf1G9UY4A%3D&reserved=0> ) is a world-class university that excels in driving innovative education, research excellence, and impactful knowledge transfer. With a holistic and interdisciplinary pedagogy approach, HKUST was ranked 3rd in the Times Higher Education‚Äôs Young University Rankings 2024, 19th Worldwide and No.1 in Hong Kong in Times Higher Education‚Äôs Impact Rankings 2025. Thirteen HKUST subjects were ranked among the world‚Äôs top 50 in the QS World University Rankings by Subject 2025, with ‚ÄúData Science and Artificial Intelligence‚Äù holding the 17th place, maintaining its position as first in Hong Kong. Our graduates are highly competitive, consistently ranking among the world‚Äôs top 30 most sought-after employees. In terms of research and entrepreneurship, over 80% of our work was rated ‚ÄúInternationally excellent‚Äù or ‚Äúworld leading‚Äù in the latest Research Assessment Exercise 2020 of Hong Kong‚Äôs University Grants Committee. As of May 2025, HKUST members have founded over 1,800 active start-ups, including 10 Unicorns and 17 exits (IPO or M&A)

Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-25 20:12:34
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: no-reply@ust.hk

Dear LI, Xueyang (21308259),



Accommodation charge for  Fall 2025-26 has been posted. Please check the charge details at the Student Information System (SIS) via myPortal (http://my.ust.hk).



The charge will be due on 4 September 2025.



Payment procedures are detailed at https://fo.hkust.edu.hk/files/fo-files/StudentPayment.pdf <https://fo.hkust.edu.hk/files/fo-files/StudentPayment.pdf>  and https://csfu.hkust.edu.hk/sites/default/files/CSFU/Guidelines%20for%20new%20payment%20method%20(WeChatPay_Alipay_FPS).pdf <https://csfu.hkust.edu.hk/sites/default/files/CSFU/Guidelines%20for%20new%20payment%20method%20(WeChatPay_Alipay_FPS).pdf> . It will take a few working days for processing and receiving your payment before records are updated on SIS; please arrange your payment early.



Students who have financial hardship can apply for deferred payment of accommodation charge at https://sfao.ust.hk/page.php?i=24#UGDefer; application has to be submitted at least 7 working days before the due date. Please contact the Scholarships and Financial Aids Office (email: sfao.fa@ust.hk <mailto:sfao.fa@ust.hk> ) for enquiries on payment deferral.



Accommodation charge paid is not refundable. If this fee is settled already, you may ignore this message.



Student Housing and Residential Life Office

The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology



==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-08-26_00-02-15-[MATH1013] Choosing the appropriate calculus course.txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: [MATH1013] Choosing the appropriate calculus course
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-26 00:02:15
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: owner-math1013-l09-fall@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

Dear students,

 

 

You are receiving this message because you have been pre-enrolled in the course MATH1013 (Calculus I) this coming Fall term.  I have already received a number of enquiries from you regarding how to decide on the appropriate first-year calculus course.  If you have similar concerns, please refer to the "important message" posted on our Canvas website:

https://canvas.ust.hk/courses/66058

 

Here is a rough guideline for choosing the calculus course that is suitable for you:

https://canvas.ust.hk/courses/66058/pages/deciding-among-different-calculus-courses

Please note that since there are some new arrangements about first-year calculus courses starting from this year, some "academic advice" that you may find online for past cohorts may no longer be valid now.  Please discuss with your academic advisor about your own program requirements.  You're also welcome to discuss with me or the course instructor of your section; we'll try to help as much as we can.

 

 

Best regards,

Henry Cheng

Coordinator of MATH1013

 

 

--



Dr. CHENG Kam Hang, Henry

Department of Mathematics

The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology

Dear all,‚ÄØ



 







 



The Diversity and Equal Opportunities Unit is delighted to invite you to join an inclusion workshop to be supported and facilitated by HSBC Hong Kong. 



 



Date and time: 2:30-4:30p.m., October 9, 2025 (A shuttle bus will be reserved to take registrants from HKUST Clear Water Bay campus at 1:45p.m. on the day.)‚ÄØ 



 



Venue: HSBC Office, HSBC Main Building, Central 



 



Language: English‚ÄØ 



 



Highlights: 



*	To learn more about inclusion and accessibility in a banking context 



*	To understand more about accessible banking, digital accessibility and community banking 



*	To learn more about HSBC‚Äôs Employee Resource Groups, network with their members and how these groups advance inclusion effort at HSBC 



 



Audience: Open to all HKUST students and staff. 



 



How to register: Please register early to reserve your seat here <https://ust.az1.qualtrics.com/jfe/form/SV_5gqXtPwtg0UzBt4>  with your HKUST email to be part of this fun learning experience. 



 



Kind reminders:  



  



*	Staff members are encouraged to check with their managers first on attendance before registration and to apply for special leave as per HKUST policy once registration is confirmed. (You can refer to guideline for special leave <https://staffmanual.hkust.edu.hk/system/files/staffs/Volunteering%20Activities%20under%20Special%20Leave.pdf?check_logged_in=1>  for more information) 



*	This is a HMAW1905-recognized event in the ‚ÄúPersonal Enrichment & Community Service" category under the "Self-directed Experience" of HMAW1905: Behavioral Foundations of University Education: Habits, Mindsets, and Wellness. To receive 2 hours, you must attend the event in full and miss no more than 10 mins. 



*	We will only arrange one-way shuttle bus to take the participants from HKUST Clear Water Bay campus to HSBC Main Building. No return transportation will be arranged.



 



We strive to host inclusive and accessible events. If you have any questions regarding the event including queries about any possibility for the event to offer any adjustments, please contact our team at deoc@ust.hk <mailto:deoc@ust.hk> .‚ÄØ‚ÄØ‚ÄØ‚ÄØ 



 



Best regards,‚ÄØ

==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-08-26_15-59-19-Join SIGHT Programs in Fall!.txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: Join SIGHT: Programs in Fall!
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-26 15:59:19
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: allug-list-request@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

 







 



 



Dear Students,



 



Greetings from SIGHT (Student Innovation for Global Health Technology)! üéâ As the new academic year approaches, we are excited to share with you some exciting news. Here are some amazing opportunities for you to revolutionize your new academic year!



 



SIGHT CAMP ‚õ∫Ô∏è



 



Join us at SIGHT Camp, a non-credit bearing program building student-led innovative projects that lasts for 8 weeks, starting in October (Thur 6pm ‚Äì 8pm), where you will confront real health-related problems and design solutions to in global communities.



 



If you are committed, creative, collaborative, and excited to make impact in the health sector, come join us! You will be EMPOWERED üí™with mindsets and skills to innovate health technologies to tackle global health issues.



 



What you will do within your projects: 



1.	Learn and apply technical skills üì±, 



2.	Grow in sustainability mindset ‚ôªÔ∏è,



3.	Encourage a human touch to the people we serve ü´Ç. 



 



The projects will primarily focus on marginalized communities in South and Southeast Asia. Successful Campers can continue their innovation as a course in Spring (UCOP3200) and collaborate with the communities to deploy your project in the Summer.



 



APPLY:  Sign-up here <https://forms.gle/Msz98Wt3pGyB5rMq6> on or before Sep 08. If you are eligible, we will be in touch for your interview later for further next steps.



 



ENGG 1300 üí≠



 



ENGG 1300 - Design Thinking for Health Innovation is a common core course, giving a taste of design thinking, offer by SIGHT.



 



This year, the theme is ‚ÄúHow to tackle stress and innovate interventions to design HKUST Life‚Äù. Everyone will work in teams, shuffled around throughout the course. Grading is based on project evaluations and multiple peer reviews.



 



SCHEDULE: Tuesday (13:30 ‚Äì 16:20)



ENROLLMENT: ‚ÄúENGG 1300‚Äù on Student Information System (SIS).



 



 



2025 Design for Global Health Competition 



 







Are you interested in not only making impact in global health but be challenged with other students worldwide and win prizes? The 2025 Design for Global Health Competition is now open for registration !



 



Organized by SIGHT and Philos Health, this initiative aims to tackle real-world public health challenges with innovative solutions designed for resource-constrained communities. University students (undergraduate & postgraduate) from the Asia-pacific regions are welcome to join the competition. 



 



INFO SESSION: September 5, 2025 (to be confirmed)



REGISTRATION DEADLINE: September 15, 2025



SUBMISSION DEADLINE: October 31, 2025 



SUBMISSION REQUIREMENTS: A 10-minute video + prototypes 



 



For more details, please visit https://competition.sight.ust.hk/ or refer to the attached poster. 



 



WANT TO FIND OUT MORE? 



 



If you want to know more about us, visit our website <https://sight2023.hkust.edu.hk/about-us> , Instagram (sight.at.hkust) for more information or email us (sight@ust.hk <mailto:sight@ust.hk> ).  



 



Cheers,



Student Innovation for Global Health Technology (SIGHT)

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: [HMAW1905 recognized] : Invitation to Join the Experience Sports Workshop and Sports Team Recruitment
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-26 16:25:21
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: Sports Development

Dear Students,



We extend a warm welcome to all new members of the HKUST community. We are delighted to have you join us and look forward to enhancing your university sports experience. To initiate your journey, we invite you to participate in our upcoming Experience Sports Workshops.

 

Join the Experience Sports Workshop

Scheduled for 28 and 29 August, the Experience Sports Workshops will be led by our esteemed HKUST Sports Tutors. You will have the opportunity to engage in at least two sports activities available at HKUST. This is an excellent chance to connect with fellow students and establish friendships with our dedicated sports leaders.

This is also a recognized event in the "Self-directed Experience" component of HMAW1905: Behavioral Foundations of University Education: Habits, Mindsets, and Wellness. You will get 2 hours if you attend the session in full.

For further details and to enrol, please click the poster or scan the QR code below.

 <https://nso.hkust.edu.hk/enrichment-activities/experience-sports-workshop> 

 

Showcase Your Sports Talents

HKUST boasts nearly 60 sports teams comprised of talented student-athletes. If you are passionate about sports, we encourage you to participate in the upcoming recruitment and training sessions for our teams in September. As a member of a sports team, you will have the opportunity to represent HKUST and showcase your athletic abilities at inter-varsity competitions.

Please click the poster below to express your sports interests and talents. We will forward all collected information to the respective team captains for their consideration.

 <https://ust.az1.qualtrics.com/jfe/form/SV_9Ex0BiMuGJFJa9E> 



Our Office of Sports Development is located at LG3002. We welcome you to visit and share your thoughts on sports promotion within our community. We are committed to supporting your athletic journey.

If you have any inquiries, please feel free to email us at sports@ust.hk or call us at 2358 8586.

Prepare to embrace the excitement of sports at HKUST!



Best regards,

Ricky Yeung

Head (Sports Development)

Dean of Students‚Äô Office

	We're back as Sew-cial Club!

Scam Alert



 



Cybersecurity Learning Series ‚Äì 



 



Why you need to protect your privacy when using free Wi-fi



 



*       Connecting to public networks opens up your phone to hackers and viruses



*       What should you do to keep your data safe if you really want to finish your YouTube video but have run out of mobile data?



 







 



How to secure your device if you really have to use public Wi-fi hotspots



 



*       Enable firewalls and antivirus software on your devices.



*       Never download or install anything while using public Wi-fi ‚Äì wait until you get home.



*       Don‚Äôt input any personal information to register for public Wi-fi. If they ask for it, don‚Äôt use this network.



*       When you finish using the public Wi-fi, always log out from the network, and click ‚ÄúForget this network‚Äù in your settings.



*       Choose your public Wi-fi wisely. Search online to check if it has been verified if you‚Äôre not sure.



*       Don‚Äôt shop online or do anything private until you switch to a secure connection.



 



Extracted from CyberDefender: https://cyberdefender.hk/en-us/why-you-need-to-protect-your-privacy-when-using-free-wi-fi/ <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcyberdefender.hk%2Fen-us%2Fwhy-you-need-to-protect-your-privacy-when-using-free-wi-fi%2F&data=05%7C02%7Cxlilv%40connect.ust.hk%7C01c5309bfe41486466c008dde4858f28%7C6c1d415239d044ca88d9b8d6ddca0708%7C1%7C0%7C638917984488825451%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=MzrC8LyEAY%2F6i4EiDwvYV4AA8MskSjBBhR0vE9NoITA%3D&reserved=0>

Dear Professors and Students,



 



The Undergraduate Research Opportunities Program (UROP) is one of the signature programs at HKUST which provides a platform for undergraduate students to engage in academic research across all disciplines under the supervision of faculty members.



 



As announced earlier, we are now calling for projects and applications for Fall 2025‚Äì26. To give you more information on the program, including the latest guidelines and policies, the eligibility requirements, project submission and application procedures, awards and sponsorships etc., an Info Session will be held with details as follows:



 



UROP Info Session (face-to-face)



Date: 2 September 2025 (Tuesday)



Time: 2pm ‚Äì 3pm



Venue: Multi -Purpose Room (Room G019), G/F, Global Graduate Tower (GGT) <https://www.google.com/maps/place/Global+Graduate+Tower+(GGT)/@22.3338937,114.2658369,17z/data=!3m1!4b1!4m6!3m5!1s0x340405b8095aeeed:0xda844baec0bbfc68!8m2!3d22.3338937!4d114.2658369!16s%2Fg%2F11qhzg9pdr?hl=en&entry=ttu&g_ep=EgoyMDI0MDkyNC4wIKXMDSoASAFQAw%3D%3D>  (please expect a 10-minute walk from the Academic Building)



 



All students and faculty members who are interested in UROP are welcome to join the session. Prior registration is required (for students only), and please register here <https://ust.az1.qualtrics.com/jfe/form/SV_esaZXKblkRZh19s>  by 31 August 2025 (Sunday).



 



Should you have any questions, please feel free to contact our office at urop@ust.hk <mailto:urop@ust.hk> . We look forward to seeing you at the Info Session.

Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-27 11:59:21
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: ece-ug-list-request@lists.ust.hk

Dear all Engineering UG students, 



 



Recruitment of STEAM Tutor Team ‚Äì October 2025 to August 2026



 



 



 



Center for Global & Community Engagement (GCE) is looking for outgoing students to work with us in STEAM Tutor Team for various STEAM activities from October 2025 to August 2026.



 



STEAM tutors who chose to join the Micro:bit sub-team will help in delivering STEAM Workshop Development to school students and general public, and Underwater Robotics with Arduino sub-team will help in development of community engagement programmes related to Underwater Robotics . 2 subteams will also work together in different STEAM programmes.



 



STEAM Tutors can gain exposure and teaching experience in STEAM workshops and meet youths from various backgrounds.



  



Below is the general timeline of application and initial training for your consideration:



 



Mon, 15 Sept 2025, 2359 : 



Application Closed



Thur, 18 Sept 2025, 1800 ‚Äì 2130 :                 



Face to Face, Group Interview (Compulsory) (30-min per session)



 



Mon, 22 Sept 2025, 1800 ‚Äì 2100 :                 



Welcome and Training Session (Compulsory) 



Mon, 29 Sept 2025 or Thur, 2 Oct 2025  1800 ‚Äì 2100 :  



Technical Skill Training for respective stream



 



 



Eligibilities



1.	Students from all disciplines are welcome to apply. 

2.	Proactive in learning basic STEAM knowledge, teaching and project development.

3.	Previous experience in helping in STEAM activities (e.g. STEAM Day@HKUST ) and teaching children science and engineering are advantages. 



4.	Available to work on weekends. 

5.	Good command of Cantonese, English, and/or Putonghua.

6.	Shortlisted candidates will be invited to attend an interview on Thur, 18 Sept 2025. 



7.	Must attend the training session in the evenings of Mon, 22 Sept 2025, Mon, 29 Sept 2025 and Thur, 2 Oct 2025.



  



 



Job Duties



1.	To develop and prepare materials for teachings and demonstrations of STEAM projects.



2.	To teach participants how to assemble the products and STEM knowledge in the workshops.

3.	To mingle with the participants and introduce them the study life at HKUST.

4.	To perform other ad-hoc tasks and provide logistical support to the workshops. 



 





Application Method for joining the team



      Application link: https://ust.az1.qualtrics.com/jfe/form/SV_3UddImODWc0gMbs



      Deadline: 23:59, Mon, 15 Sept 2025



 



 



For any enquiries, please feel free to contact us at gce@ust.hk <mailto:gce@ust.hk>  .



 



Thank you.



 



Best regards, 



Center for Global & Community Engagement (GCE)



School of Engineering 



The Hong Kong University of Science & Technology 



Instagram: @hkust.seng.gce



https://www.instagram.com/hkust.seng.gce/ <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.instagram.com%2Fhkust.seng.gce%2F&data=05%7C02%7Cxlilv%40connect.ust.hk%7C919d36bfc82e4047cbc708dde51e1772%7C6c1d415239d044ca88d9b8d6ddca0708%7C1%7C0%7C638918639613350510%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=0LprKb3t1ApU53ceLFtmZte3iR00L73g7dzZxz%2FTyVQ%3D&reserved=0> 



==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-08-27_14-27-38-Welcome to a New Academic Year at HKUST.txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: Welcome to a New Academic Year at HKUST
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-27 14:27:38
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: allug-list-request@lists.ust.hk

To: All Undergraduate and Postgraduate Students



cc: All faculty and teaching staff



---------------------------------------------------------------



 



Dear Students,



 



A heartfelt welcome to each of you! Whether you are returning to campus or joining us for the first time, we are truly delighted to have you as part of the HKUST community. You are valued members of our community, and your presence enriches our vibrant and diverse university.



 



As we step into a new academic year starting next Monday (September 1), the campus will once again be alive with energy, curiosity, and excitement. We‚Äôre looking forward to the incredible mix of backgrounds, experiences, and talents that all of you, returning, new first-year, and exchange-in students, bring to our community.



 



At HKUST, we believe that education is not just about academic achievement, but also about personal growth, collaboration, and mutual respect. We encourage you to engage fully in campus life, support one another, and appreciate the diverse perspectives that make our university unique. Our goal is to foster an inclusive and supportive environment where everyone can thrive.



 



We are committed to open communication and are always here to listen to your ideas and concerns. Should you have any questions or need guidance, please feel free to reach out to us, your home department/division, or consult the resources available on the Dean of Students‚Äô Office website <https://dst.hkust.edu.hk/eng/detail.php?catid=42&sid=338> .



 



As you embark on your academic journey, we would also like to remind you of the importance of academic integrity - one of HKUST‚Äôs core values. Upholding honesty and responsibility in your studies ensures that we all contribute to the excellence and reputation of our university. You can find important information and guidelines in the following resources:



 



*	Undergraduate Student Guide <https://registry.hkust.edu.hk/resource-library/undergraduate-student-guide-0> 

*	Handbook for Research Postgraduate Studies <https://fytgs.hkust.edu.hk/academics/Academic-Regulations-and-Requirements/Handbook-for-Research-Postgraduate-Studies/preface> 

*	Handbook for Taught Postgraduate Studies <https://fytgs.hkust.edu.hk/academics/Academic-Regulations-and-Requirements/Handbook-for-Taught-Postgraduate-Studies/preface> 



 



We are excited to see the campus come alive with your ideas, energy, and enthusiasm. Let us make this year a memorable and inspiring one together!



 



Once again, welcome to HKUST. We wish you every success and happiness in the coming year.



 



 



Best regards,



 



 



Yike Guo, Provost

Jimmy Fung, Associate Provost (Teaching & Learning)

Check-in Reminder



 



Residential period start:



28 August 2025



Check-in during: 



From 10:00, 28 August 2025 to 22:00, 4 September 2025 (HKT)



 



 



Late Check-in



If you are unable to check-in by the stated deadline, you must email your hall office and ughousing@ust.hk, providing your reason and relevant proof to request for special arrangement. Otherwise, you will NOT be allowed to check-in upon arrival and may risk having your Hall Offer CANCELLED without prior notice. At the same time, you will still be held accountable for the hall charges, and the paid hall fees will NOT be refunded.



 



 



Check-in Procedures



Check-in details are available here: https://shrl.hkust.edu.hk/residential-halls/hall-life/check-in-out-procedures.

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: Check-In Room Condition Record Submission

Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: shrloinfo@ust.hk

Dear LI, Xueyang (SID: 21308259),



Please click this link <https://studenthousing.hkust.edu.hk/page/rcr>  OR scan the QR code attached in your room card holder to get access to room condition record form. Please check your room facilities and furniture based on the list and mark down the condition in the form. You should submit the form to us within 7 days upon your check-in date.



If you cannot activate your HKUST network account to submit the above form within 7 days. You may click here <https://studenthousingsuppt.hkust.edu.hk/>  to login with your HKID/Passport No./Appl. No. instead.



You will only be allowed to submit room condition record form within 7 days upon your check-in. If you fail to submit the form on or before the 7th day upon your check in, it is assumed that the items in your room/apartment stated in this the room condition list are in good condition and your access to the form will be terminated. You and/or your roommate(s) will be held responsible when the items on the list are found damaged/missing upon check-out.



If you have difficulties in accessing the form, please email to hallmanage@ust.hk <mailto:hallmanage@ust.hk?subject=Enquiry%20on%20the%20online%20room%20condition%20record%20form>  for assistance.



Thank you for your attention and cooperation.



Regards,

Student Housing and Residential Life Office

Workshop







	

Mosaic Alumni Sharing Series - Thriving Academically and Culturally: Postgraduate Life in the UK



	

This alumni-led session offers participants insights into postgraduate study in the UK, including academic expectations, learning styles, and assessments. It also provides tips on adapting to UK life, socializing, handling challenges, and embracing the culture. Whether applying or not, participants will gain practical advice and personal stories to enhance their UK experience. 



Speaker: Alvin Ng <http://www.linkedin.com/in/alvinth>

==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-08-29_11-41-30-[Online & F2F] Mental Health First Aid Courses for Students (Fall 202526) .txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: [Online & F2F] Mental Health First Aid Courses for Students (Fall 2025/26) 
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-08-29 11:41:30
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: counsel-info-request@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

Dear Students,



Hope you are staying healthy and well.    



The World Health Organization(WHO) states that mental health is an integral and essential component of health.  It was estimated worldwide that up to 20% of children and adolescents experience various severity of mental disorders. In order to equip our university community with knowledge and skills to address mental health concerns, we are pleased to deliver a 12-hour Mental Health First Aid course <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmhfa.com.au%2F&data=05%7C02%7Cxlilv%40connect.ust.hk%7Cf14aedc6a7674cacb59d08dde6aded1f%7C6c1d415239d044ca88d9b8d6ddca0708%7C1%7C0%7C638920356897246766%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=HXlvkXcgCaEA%2FoCmr6sBZkictpf1r2erCC0pvth8Y%2FE%3D&reserved=0>  to all students and faculty/staff on a regular basis.  In the past decade, over 2,500 students and 700 faculty/staff have completed this course and become Mental Health First Aiders. We highly encourage you to participate in this course if you would like to take part in building a healthier place for the community.  You may find the details of the course below.



Our joint effort is crucial for building a caring, nurturing and stigma-free learning environment.



Counseling and Wellness Center

Dean of Students' Office



 



If you cannot view this email properly, please click here <https://counsel.hkust.edu.hk/public_uploads/MHFASTUD25.png> . 







*** Take Good Care.  Stay Healthy. ***



If you notice that your psychological health is deteriorating, we highly encourage you to talk to our Student Counselors by calling us at 2358 6696 or sending us an email counsel@ust.hk <mailto:counsel@ust.hk> .  You may also visit our website <https://counsel.hkust.edu.hk/index.php>  to learn more about our counseling resources or call our 24/7 HEARing at 8208 2688, which is a 24-hour helpline exclusively for all HKUST students 7 days a week.  The service is made available by our Counselors in collaboration with the Christian Family Service Center <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cfsc.org.hk%2Fen&data=05%7C02%7Cxlilv%40connect.ust.hk%7Cf14aedc6a7674cacb59d08dde6aded1f%7C6c1d415239d044ca88d9b8d6ddca0708%7C1%7C0%7C638920356897299732%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=Mg9kHDya2hoWQlGBlhS2RtyNL3mV9i5OZafY5usUL3c%3D&reserved=0> . [The following message is for all NEW students (UG & PG).]



 



 



Dear New Students,



 



Welcome to HKUST! We hope you had a restful summer break. 



 



We write to alert you of a mandatory requirement for all NEW students ‚Äì the Anti-scam Challenge (ASCM1000). You must complete and ‚ÄúPass‚Äù (50% correct) the challenge by 21 Sep 2025 for continued access to Library resources (all electronic resources and physical access) beyond 21 Sep 2025.



 



ASCM1000 will be accessible via Canvas <https://canvas.ust.hk/> , starting 1 Sep 2025. It contains 15 random multiple-choice questions. This is to equip students with essential information against scams and fraud, a top crime world-wide as technology advances. According to local government statistics, students are often targets of scammers. 



 



If you complete and pass the challenge after the 21 Sep 2025 due date, access to the library may take up to two workdays to resume. For enquiries, please contact the Dean of Students‚Äô Office at antiscam@ust.hk <mailto:antiscam@ust.hk> . 



 



We would also like to share the following from the Hong Kong Government with you: 



*	Message from the Commissioner of Police on Scam Prevention <https://dst.hkust.edu.hk/upload/resources/Message_the_Commissioner_of_Poli.pdf> 

*	HK Anti-Deception Coordination Centre (ADCC) webpage on the latest scam tricks <https://www.adcc.gov.hk/en-hk/alerts.html> 



 



Most importantly, if you are in doubt, seek help. Call ADCC‚Äôs helpline at 18222 or email us at antiscam@ust.hk <mailto:antiscam@ust.hk> . Let‚Äôs be scam-smart and join hands in supporting each other for a scam-free campus!



 



Regards,



Dean of Students‚Äô Office



29 Aug 2025

The following message is intended for undergraduate students in Fall Term 2025-26



 



 



Dear Undergraduate Students



 



The Fall Term 2025-26 will start on 1 September 2025 (next Monday).  Please check your updated class enrollment records with the SIS (Student Center).  Refer to 'My Class Schedule' for the wait-listing and enrolled classes in both list and weekly calendar views.  You may filter the Enrolled, Waitlisted and Dropped classes in the schedule.



 



Due to system routine maintenance and the release of reserved quotas, the Class Enrollment functions (add/drop/swap and the shopping cart) will be SUSPENDED from 11:59pm, 31 August (Sunday) to 9:30am, 1 September 2025 (Monday).  Students who wish to submit add/drop requests before the start of term are advised to complete their requests by 11:59pm, 31 August.  Checking of ‚ÄúMy Class Schedule‚Äù will not be affected and is available throughout the term.



 



The last day of Add/Drop period of most undergraduate classes is 13 September 2025 (Saturday).  The add/drop/swap functions will close at 11:59pm on that day.  For the wait-listing classes, a place may be confirmed automatically any time during the add/drop period when vacancies arise.  Please check your class enrollment records frequently.  If you no longer want to enroll in the classes you are waiting, you must DROP the 'waiting' classes yourself.  Around 1:00am each day, email notifications will be sent to students whose waiting class has been confirmed on the previous day.



 



Please be reminded again that classes in your shopping cart are not yet confirmed.  You need to enroll the classes before the end of add/drop if you want to take the classes.



 



Let us know if you have any questions.  Please always quote your student number and full name in your e-mail enquiries.  Thank you.

Dear UST members,



Are you ready for another exciting semester at HKUST? What better way to enhance your skills and expand your horizons than by exploring the free online courses available through our MOOC partner, Coursera?

*	access to a wealth of knowledge through extensive program catalogs

*	earn FREE certificates to showcase your skills



We are excited to offer you two fantastic programs:



	 

 	 Program	  	 What is it?	  	 For Whom?

Joining these programs is easy! Just follow these steps:



1.	Go to the program page and click ‚ÄúJoin‚Äù.

2.	In the ‚ÄúLog In‚Äù box, select  Log in with HKUST at the top.

3.	On the HKUST credential page, enter your @connect.ust.hk or @ust.hk account and password (DO NOT use your email alias)

4.	Once logged in, browse the course catalog and enroll in any courses that interest you.

5.	Complete course requirements to earn FREE certificates!



Important Note: These courses are non-credit bearing and are intended for your personal interest and development. However, that doesn‚Äôt make them any less exciting though ‚Äî take full advantage of this opportunity to learn something new!



If you have any questions, there are plenty of resources available:



*	Check out Coursera‚Äôs Help Articles on how to join a learning program <https://www.coursera.support/s/article/115001710066-Join-a-learning-program?language=en_US>  first.

*	Contact Coursera's Learner Help Center <https://www.coursera.support/s/learner-help-center?language=en_US>  or post a question in Coursera‚Äôs Community Help <https://www.coursera.support/s/community?language=en_US> .

Dear Students,



 



Welcome (back) to HKUST! Great to see many of you on campus again. Career Center is ready to engage and support you on your journey of career planning, internship and graduate job search. Check out what we have on offer!



 



Career Consultation



 <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/page.php?section=meet_advisors> 



Need help with CV writing? Not sure how you can land an internship? Can‚Äôt figure out how to navigate a challenging job market? Come meet our career advisors! We are here to help you discuss any career-related issues. We are also excited to announce that our guest career consultants will be available in Sep 2025 to provide career consultation sessions for all of you. Bookings can be made two weeks in advance on our online Consultation Appointment Chart <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/schedule.php> . Walk-ins are also welcome!



 



Recruitment Events



Many employers are eager to hire HKUST students! Different types of recruitment talks and events are happening this term. Check them out under Recruitment Events <http://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/page.php?sid=47>  and sign up!



 <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/page.php?sid=47> 



 



Graduate Jobs and Internships



 <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/job.php> 



Our HKUST-exclusive Job Board <http://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/job.php>  is the one-stop career portal for employers to post their job openings when they look for HKUST students and graduates! You can also visit Joint Institutions Job Information System (JIJIS) <http://www.jijis.org.hk/>  to look for full-time, part-time, temporary and winter/summer jobs, accessible to students from all UGC funded tertiary institutions in Hong Kong. There are also many third-party Internship Programs <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/page.php?sid=74>  offering internships across local, mainland and overseas destinations. Many of these opportunities are open to all students, including 1st and 2nd year undergraduates. Check them out!



 



Co-op Program



Career Center offers a university-wide co-op program <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/page.php?sid=89> , a unique opportunity to integrate academic learning with hands-on work experience in some of our most popular employers for our undergraduate students. Participating students are required to apply for study leave and take up a full-time co-op placement for a period of at least 4 months. After completion of the co-op internship, students would enroll in a 3-credit co-op course in the following semester. Check out the co-op opportunities on our HKUST-exclusive Job Board <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/job.php?keywords=&EMT%5B%5D=13>  now!



 <https://career.hkust.edu.hk/web/page.php?sid=89>

1. Career Building Course and 2. Designing Your Life

==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-09-01_10-32-59-A Warm Welcome to HKUST Engineering Students.txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: A Warm Welcome to HKUST Engineering Students
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-09-01 10:32:59
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: ece-ug-list-request@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

 



	

	

  



 <https://t.radica.ust.hk/activities_web/sample/click?msgid=06d0619c-a671-41b8-8232-ea979ab5324a&linkid=612e0c27180f680001348b53> 



 <https://images.radica.ust.hk/resource/campaign/612e02f1180f680001348b0c/images/9A4dH_line-1.png> 



 <https://t.radica.ust.hk/activities_web/sample/click?msgid=06d0619c-a671-41b8-8232-ea979ab5324a&linkid=612e0c27180f680001348b54> 









  



 <https://images.radica.ust.hk/resource/campaign/68b4f4540d412f00016df45b/images/ZkRyS0RfV2VsY29tZSBhbGwgRW5naW5lZXJpbmcgc3R1ZGVudHNfcmFkaWNhLnBuZw%3D%3D> 



Dear students,



Welcome to the 2025-26 academic year. It is with great joy that I greet you on this first day of school. This year we are excited to admit a record high of nearly 1,100 new undergraduate students, with around one-third of them coming from an impressive diversity of 29 countries and regions, including new additions from Belarus, Cambodia, Ethiopia, Jamaica, Rwanda, and Yemen. Similarly, we have admitted a record number of over 500 research postgraduate students and 1,600 full-time and part-time MSc students. Thank you for your trust in HKUST as the place to build your future. Together, we live out our motto, ‚ÄúEngineering Our Future!‚Äù

 

This year also marks a significant change in our undergraduate admissions process, with a good portion of you being admitted directly into your departments. This department-based admission allows you an early start to follow a tailored pathway specific to your chosen department, while the school-based admission provides you with the flexibility to explore various fields ‚Äì offering the best of both worlds.

 

To enhance your learning experience, we have established a new leadership position for an Executive Director for Undergraduate Recruitment and Student Development in this academic year. This role is dedicated to strengthening our engagement with industry partners, creating more collaboration and internship opportunities for you. With joining forces of our leadership team of Associate Deans, Center/Program Directors, Department Heads, we are committed to enriching your experience and helping you fulfill your aspirations. 

 

Your university years may be one of the most memorable years of your life or the most critical years for your personal and professional development. As you embark on this journey, I encourage you to explore and grow beyond the classroom. From exchanges to internships, competitions to student organizations, volunteering to leadership training, each of these experiences will enrich your education and help you discover your passions and strengths.

 

As you transition to a new environment and stage of life, it is absolutely normal at times to feel frustrated and lost. Many students experience these feelings, and I want to let you know that you are not alone. Whether it‚Äôs reaching out to your friends, connecting with peer mentors, or talking to our dedicated wellness team staff, faculty members, or academic advisors, there are many people here who genuinely care and want to support you. So step out and don‚Äôt hesitate to lean on us. We‚Äôll help you navigate this journey and discover yourself.

 

The Engineering Commons ‚Äì our ‚Äúhome‚Äù and vibrant hub has truly become a cornerstone of our community for hosting a number of major events. I encourage you to make the most of the Commons and participate in activities there for socializing, learning and collaborating throughout your years at HKUST.

 

As a key champion in transforming engineering education, we are committed to nurturing your growth. A heartfelt welcome again to each of you. May your time at HKUST be fulfilling and unforgettable! See you around!



Sincerely,

Prof. Hong K. LO

Dean of Engineering

Dear students,



 



Welcome to a new academic year! Hope you are enjoying your first week back to school. With the start of a new school year, Be Our Guest @HKUST is looking for committed and passionate students to be part of our team!



 



ABOUT US



Established in 2015, Be Our Guest @HKUST is a student-led initiative supported by the HKUST Office of Global Learning. We provide a platform to connect local and international students to promote cultural diversity and facilitate in-depth cultural exchange experiences.



 



What you can get from joining Be Our Guest @HKUST:



*	Develop valuable hard and soft skills relating to your team of choice

*	Gain additional exposure to cultural diversity

*	Make and work with new friends from different backgrounds and expand your social network



 



INTERESTED IN JOINING US? 



We‚Äôve prepared an Application Package <https://drive.google.com/file/d/1o91_TZ6POriBLmNehWKbgovzWU4Z3FAI/view>  for you to learn more about us and the roles available. If you are interested in joining us, please fill in the online application form on or before 23:59 (GMT+8) 12th September 2025. A confirmation email and interview time slot will be sent to you by 17th September 2025, should you be shortlisted for an interview.

==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-09-01_11-52-17-[Student] Tips on ELEC191029103910.txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: [Student] Tips on ELEC1910/2910/3910
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-09-01 11:52:17
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: owner-elec1910-t15-fall@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

Dear ELEC1910/2910/3910 students,



 



Welcome to the academic year 2025-26!



 



ELEC1910 (for 2025-26 intake onwards), ELEC2910, ELEC3910 are compulsory one-year Academic and Professional Development courses for BEng in Electronic Engineering students. These courses are designed to provide academic advising to students and/or to develop students' communication skills in interacting with the technical and non-technical audiences in their professional careers.



 



To help you survive in these courses, we prepared a ‚ÄúTips on ELEC1910/2910/3910‚Äù as attached for your information. 



 



We strongly recommend you meet with your faculty advisor by the end of the add-drop period. Please contact your faculty advisor accordingly to make an appointment with him/her in advance. You can find your tutorial group and faculty advisor on SIS. 



 



A detailed course arrangement will be sent to you after the add/drop period. Please stay tuned for our updates. 



 



Thank you for your attention.



 



Best regards,



Suki YUEN



ECE

==================== [ÂÜÖÂÆπÊù•Ê∫ê: 2025-09-01_13-05-54-[UG Hall VI] Reminder on Turnstile InOut and Visitor Policy.txt] ====================

‰∏ªÈ¢ò: [UG Hall VI] Reminder on Turnstile In/Out and Visitor Policy
Êó∂Èó¥: 2025-09-01 13:05:54
Âèë‰ª∂‰∫∫: ughvi-allresidents-request@lists.ust.hk
--------------------Ê≠£Êñá--------------------

Dear residents,

 

Kindly note that all residents shall enter/leave hall through turnstile every time by tapping your HKUST card on the reader as below: 

 



 

According to our current hall policy, one resident could bring in two visitors at a time. A resident may invite visitors to the Hall during the visitor hours, 9:00 a.m. - 11:00 p.m. The host resident needs to escort the visitor to register electronically at the pair-up reader, and accompany the visitor in person at all times within the hall premises, including at the collection and return of Visitor Card at the Reception. The host resident will be held responsible for the conduct and safety of the visitor, or any charges or damages incurred by the visitor while s/he is in the Hall. 

 

Attached is the pair-up instruction for your information. ‚Äã

 

Regards,

Hall Office, UG Hall VI

Invitation to Join HK Electric Green Energy Dreams Come True 2025/26 (Tertiary Institutes)



 



Organised by HK Electric, Green Energy Dreams Come True, is a competition designed to promote research and innovation in green energy, carbon reduction, and sustainability. The programme also recognises outstanding student projects that demonstrate excellence in these areas.



 



Awards



*	Each shortlisted project will receive a seed fund of up to HK$50,000 to support its research and implementation. 

*	The Champion team will be awarded a cash prize of HK$30,000 and a study tour in Mainland China on green energy development. 

*	The 1st and 2nd runner up team will receive a cash prize of HK$20,000 and HK$10,000 respectively.



 



Eligibility



*	The competition is open to higher diploma, associate degree, and bachelor‚Äôs degree students from tertiary institutions in Hong Kong. 

*	Students may apply individually or in teams of up to four members.

If you can‚Äôt read this email, click here <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2Fnews%2Fhkust-salutes-gbas-top-global-innovation-ranking&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7C21e82197fb6e4e8b5f1008dde9491de6%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638923222428030091%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=KBTJwmebIneyxFyxarmxgt6K2jONQh3FvrlOZIk9duo%3D&reserved=0>  



	

 



	

 <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2F&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7C21e82197fb6e4e8b5f1008dde9491de6%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638923222428057976%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=8U0b%2F1Vmk3ELr3PFCi0D0%2B6AA2Opk%2F0RlZed%2Bg1teH8%3D&reserved=0> 



	

	

HKUST Salutes GBA's Top Global Innovation Ranking



	

	

2025-09-01



	



 <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2Fsites%2Fdefault%2Ffiles%2Fnews%2F23889%2F%252BWAL0818_r_0_0_0_1.jpg&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7C21e82197fb6e4e8b5f1008dde9491de6%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638923222428073630%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=YEtERAd7Hcg%2B%2BDdQlpPdqjv4GHZwUTfAa5ZPiCmNB14%3D&reserved=0> 



	

HKUST President Prof. Nancy IP



	



The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology (HKUST) today extended its warmest congratulations to the nation and the Guangdong-Hong Kong-Macao Greater Bay Area (GBA) for the exceptional performance in the World Intellectual Property Organization (WIPO) 2025 Global Innovation Index (GII). The "Shenzhen-Hong Kong-Guangzhou" cluster has been ranked the 1st largest innovation cluster in the Global Innovation Index 2025 top 100 ranking, ascending from its previous position and marking a historic achievement. This rise to the top is underscored by exceptional performance metrics, with the cluster filing 2,292 Patent Cooperation Treaty (PCT) applications, publishing 3,775 scientific articles, and securing 135 venture capital deals‚Äîall per 1 million inhabitants over the past five years. This data reflects the cluster‚Äôs unparalleled growth and dynamic capacity for world-leading innovation.



The sustained excellence also underscores the powerful synergy and collaborative spirit within the GBA. The ranking, which this year expanded its criteria to include venture capital activity alongside patent applications and scientific publications, provides a comprehensive validation of the cluster's robust innovation ecosystem. It recognizes not only "quantitative" outputs but also "qualitative" strengths in higher education, international talent attraction, and strong capital market support.



The WIPO GII 2025 event was a significant honor for Hong Kong, marking the first time the city hosted the prestigious Global Innovation Index Science and Technology Cluster Launch. The event featured high-level panel discussions, including one titled "Greater Bay Area‚Äôs Innovation Strengths and Future Potential," moderated by HKUST President Prof. Nancy IP, and another titled "Leading Clusters from Other World Regions," moderated by Mr. Marco ALEMAN, Assistant Director General of WIPO.



In her opening address, Prof. Ip stated: "Hong Kong is exceptionally honored and thrilled to host this prestigious event for the first time. It highlights Hong Kong‚Äôs significance both as a core city of the Greater Bay Area and as a global innovation and technology hub."



She further emphasized the region's strategic importance: "The Greater Bay Area (GBA) plays a strategically important role in the nation's scientific and technological innovation system, a status clearly evidenced by its performance in the Global Innovation Index. After ranking second globally for five consecutive years, the Shenzhen-Hong Kong-Guangzhou cluster has now risen to claim the top position. This achievement underscores the GBA's role as a leading global performer in both innovation and economic impact. I believe this success is driven by its comprehensive innovation ecosystem, which comprises robust R&D capabilities, advanced industries, a large and dynamic market, strategic investments, solid infrastructure, sound government policy and regulation, and ample funding."



The panel of experts then delivered deeper insights into these key drivers, exploring the region‚Äôs world-class R&D capabilities, the strategic deployment of ‚Äúventure capital,‚Äù and the dynamic growth of its startup community. Discussions highlighted the essential policies shaping the cluster‚Äôs success‚Äîincluding those related to talent attraction, financial incentives, intellectual property protection, and cross-border collaboration. The panel also examined the evolving role of universities in advancing frontier research, facilitating commercialization, and cultivating high-level talent, as well as the growing importance of international partnerships in guiding the cluster‚Äôs future development.





HKUST: An Engine of Innovation in the GBA Cluster





As a cornerstone of this top-ranked cluster, HKUST‚Äôs contributions are deeply woven into the fabric of the GBA‚Äôs innovation ecosystem. The University is a prolific generator of high-impact knowledge, consistently ranked first in the Nature Index for patent influence within China and boasting an exceptionally high patent utilization rate. This strong performance ensures that its research continues to create tangible economic and social value.



HKUST‚Äôs culture of innovation has directly nurtured a new generation of industry leaders. Its alumni and faculty are the driving force behind multiple GBA unicorns and tech giants, including global leader DJI, industrial automation powerhouse Googol Tech, Intelligent vision product leader APT Electronics, advanced smart manufacturing innovator SmartMore, a HK listed mobile sports simulation games developer GALA Sports and Zhuhai's rising star Yunzhou Tech.



This entrepreneurial pipeline is powered by the University‚Äôs robust support system, which includes four established incubators: InnoBay@CWB in Hong Kong, the Blue Bay Incubator in Shenzhen, the Guangdong-HK-Macau (International) Youth Entrepreneur Hub in Guangzhou, and the HKUST Foshan Center for Technology Transfer and Commercialization in Foshan.



These physical hubs are complemented by comprehensive academic programs, including experiential-based learning for undergraduates and the master‚Äôs program in Technology Leadership and Entrepreneurship (TLE) under the Academy of Interdisciplinary Studies‚Äô Division of Integrative Systems and Design (ISD). Together, these initiatives are designed to nurture the next generation of entrepreneurs and innovators, equipping them to work across disciplines and develop disruptive innovations that address pressing societal challenges.



‚ÄúThe GBA‚Äôs top ranking is a resounding validation of our collective efforts,‚Äù said Prof. Nancy Ip in her concluding remarks. ‚ÄúSince its founding, HKUST has placed strong emphasis on innovation and entrepreneurship, serving as an active engine for the innovation ecosystem. We have contributed significantly to the GBA‚Äôs growth story through high-impact patents‚Äîwith a utilization rate of 30%‚Äîas well as an unparalleled record of nurturing unicorns, and incubators and ISD programs that empower tomorrow‚Äôs entrepreneurs. We will continue to leverage these strengths to solidify the GBA‚Äôs role as a leading international innovation hub.‚Äù



The University remains dedicated to fostering the cross-disciplinary research and international cooperation necessary to unlock the next chapter of the GBA's innovation story.

About The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology 

The Hong Kong University of Science and Technology (HKUST) (https://hkust.edu.hk/ <https://apc01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhkust.edu.hk%2F&data=05%7C02%7Cmedia%40ust.hk%7C21e82197fb6e4e8b5f1008dde9491de6%7Cc917f3e2932249269bb3daca730413ca%7C1%7C0%7C638923222428122384%7CUnknown%7CTWFpbGZsb3d8eyJFbXB0eU1hcGkiOnRydWUsIlYiOiIwLjAuMDAwMCIsIlAiOiJXaW4zMiIsIkFOIjoiTWFpbCIsIldUIjoyfQ%3D%3D%7C0%7C%7C%7C&sdata=0UTEvwIMIKEY12SYffKp9B4yuKCV%2FRQdaIuyw%2BvoNSw%3D&reserved=0> ) is a world-class university that excels in driving innovative education, research excellence, and impactful knowledge transfer. With a holistic and interdisciplinary pedagogy approach, HKUST was ranked 3rd in the Times Higher Education‚Äôs Young University Rankings 2024, 19th Worldwide and No.1 in Hong Kong in Times Higher Education‚Äôs Impact Rankings 2025. Thirteen HKUST subjects were ranked among the world‚Äôs top 50 in the QS World University Rankings by Subject 2025, with ‚ÄúData Science and Artificial Intelligence‚Äù holding the 17th place, maintaining its position as first in Hong Kong. Our graduates are highly competitive, consistently ranking among the world‚Äôs top 30 most sought-after employees. In terms of research and entrepreneurship, over 80% of our work was rated ‚ÄúInternationally excellent‚Äù or ‚Äúworld leading‚Äù in the latest Research Assessment Exercise 2020 of Hong Kong‚Äôs University Grants Committee. As of July 2025, HKUST members have founded over 1,900 active start-ups, including 10 Unicorns and 17 exits (IPO or M&A)
